The guest room is not large, with half of the bathroom and half of the bedroom. The shower room is well sealed, and the handheld shower and tropical rainforest shower have sufficient water output. With large bottles of bathing products, it is comfortable to take a bath! A hot spring pool is installed under the window facing east, and you can release the hot spring by turning on the faucet. It is a comfortable life to soak in hot springs and drink Green Yangchun every day! The bedding is of excellent quality, delicate and soft to the touch, clean and skin-friendly, and has a good sleeping experience. Zui Yangzhou is the hotel's all-day restaurant (three meals a day), with a rich variety of breakfasts and good taste. The main meals of Yangzhou fried rice, crab meat and dried silk, and Wang tofu are all delicious, of course, the price is not low. The hotel is not far from the East Gate of the Slender West Lake Scenic Area, which is very convenient. This is a hotel suitable for vacation, a great hotel!

In the hotel, you can experience the Zen teahouse, enjoy the ducks of the West Lake coming ashore to eat, and overlook the Daming Temple Tower. You can cross the road to the Qianmu Sports Park to see the Song City Wall and walk for fitness.

Let me talk about the disadvantages first. I hope the hotel can improve and enhance the guest experience.
1. The privacy is too poor. First of all, the hot spring pool (Figure 2) is really too outdoor. It is separated by a fence. I dare not try it unless it is dark. Secondly, people living on the second floor can directly see the bathroom on the first floor. Although there are electric blackout curtains, when the guests on the first floor come back at night, it is pitch black from the indoors to the outdoors, but it is really clear from the outdoors to the indoors (as shown in Figure 9). It is recommended that the hotel can remind residents to remember to close the curtains at the electric curtains, just like the sticker on the door to remember to lock it, or put a frosted sticker on the glass of the shower room.
2. Is there an SOP to check when the cleaning aunt is cleaning? When preparing to make tea, I found that there were tea leaves left by the previous guest in the teapot.
3. There are a few varieties of breakfast. As a resort hotel, it is a bit disappointing.
„ÄêAdvantages„Äë

It feels very comfortable to walk along the lake in the morning.

The refreshments and tea were quite good, and the price was also very reasonable, 100/person (2 types) Tea set) or 150/person (three tea sets). If you focus on leisure travel, I think it is perfect to live here.
In addition, there are Yangzhou Banquet and Xiangyuan Tea House within a 500-meter walk of the hotel. You can queue up to eat at different times. The food in the hotel's own restaurant is also very delicious. It may not be top-notch, but it is better than the long queue outside. You feel more at ease when stepping on thunder. It is suitable to live here with the elderly and children.
